08/12/21, 1:45 pm - codeAj: class Solution:
    def lengthOfLongestSubstring(self, s: str) -> int:
        if len(s) == 1:
            aj=1
            return aj
        else :
            seet=set()
            s=s[1:]
            aj=0
            for i in s:
                seet.add(i)
                aj=len(seet)
            return aj
